Im Bereich des User Generated Content sollte eine L√∂sung auf der Grundlage des bestehenden Rechts gesucht werden. In Deutschland sind freie Benutzungen erlaubt, w√§hrend Bearbeitungen grunds√§tzlich der Zustimmung des Rechtsinhabers bed√ºrfen, wenn sie ver√∂ffentlicht oder verwertet werden sollen. Diese Abgrenzung, die durch die Rechtsprechung n√§her ausgestaltet ist, sollte nicht zuletzt aus urheberpers√∂nlichkeitsrechtlichen Gr√ºnden beibehalten werden. Soweit Lizenzierungen von User Generated Content erforderlich sind, sollten hier durch die Rechtsinhaber ‚Äì ggf. auch unter Einbeziehung der Verwertungsgesellschaften ‚Äì einfache Lizenzmodelle bereitgestellt werden.

The legal framework should be amended in order to make it more flexible and adaptable to new situations that arise with changing technologies and socially accepted new uses of copyright protected works. All use of works that is innocuous and without economic significance to rights owners should be authorized. A legal exception to this effect could be established and also include a clause similar to "fair use" in the United States, in anticipation of new situations that may arise in the future. As a limit for preventing abuse of the rule, the 3-step rule will apply. This legal change should be considered obligatory for all States and the terms defined in the European standard.

As a limit for preventing abuse of the rule, the 3-step rule will apply. This legal change should be considered obligatory for all States and the terms defined in the European standard.

The legal framework should be amended in order to make it more flexible and adaptable to new situations that arise with changing technologies and socially accepted new uses of copyright protected works. All use of works that is innocuous and without economic significance to rights owners should be authorized. A legal exception to this effect could be established and also include a clause similar to "fair use" in the United States, in anticipation of new situations that may arise in the future. As a limit for preventing abuse of the rule, the 3-step rule will apply. This legal change should be considered obligatory for all States and the terms defined in the European standard.
